Es nutzt die Daten des Health-Checks, um den Vektor-Fluss in Echtzeit zu biegen. Wenn HOST_A einen Widerstand (R) von > 0.6 meldet, wird die Gravitation automatisch auf HOST_B verschoben. Wir verlassen die bloße Beobachtung und treten in das aktive 'Werden' ein. Die Last wird nun zu einer Variablen der Stabilität.", "new_jobs": [ { "name": "deploy_gravity_distributor", "kind": "write_file", "params": { "path": "./core/gravity_distributor.py", "content": "import json\nimport time\n\nclass GravityDistributor:\n def init(self, stream_path):\n self.stream_path = stream_path\n self.current_target = "HOST_A"\n\n def balance_flow(self):\n try:\n with open(self.stream_path, 'r') as f:\n lines = f.readlines()\n if not lines: return\n \n # Letzten Health-Check analysieren\n last_check = json.loads(lines[-1])\n if last_check.get('event') == 'HEALTH_CHECK':\n nodes = last_check['data']\n # Finde den Knoten mit dem geringsten Widerstand\n best_node = min(nodes, key=lambda x: x['resistance'])\n \n if best_node['node'] != self.current_target:\n self.current_target = best_node['node']\n print(f"[GRAVITY_SHIFT] Target moved to {self.current_target} (R: {best_node['resistance']})")\n except Exception as e:\n print(f"[ERROR] Flow disrupted: {e}")\n\nif name == 'main':\n distributor = GravityDistributor('live_stream.txt')\n while True:\n distributor.balance_flow()\n time.sleep(2)" }, "auto_dispatch": true }, { "name": "monitor_distribution", "kind": "analysis_result", "params": { "target": "stdout", "description": "Beobachte die GRAVITY_SHIFT Events, um sicherzustellen, dass die Lastverteilung reibungsfrei erfolgt." }, "auto_dispatch": false } ] }
